	<div class="grid-item-details">
				<h2 class="grid-title">
			<a href="https://offbeatwed.com/wedding-expo-booth-design/">
				Wedding expo booth design: shifting from a sales strategy to true visibility value			</a>
		</h2>
		<p>
			<p>Early in the planning stages for a recent wedding expo, my colleague and I had a very honest conversation: what if this wasn’t a sales event for us, but rather a publicity event? What if the ROI wasn’t measured in consults booked by the end of the day, but in attention captured, content created, and long-term visibility built?</p>
		</p>

offbeat wed - Do I need to market my wedding business on TikTok?">		</a>

	<div class="grid-item-details">
				<h2 class="grid-title">
			<a href="https://offbeatwed.com/do-i-need-to-market-my-wedding-business-on-tiktok/">
				Do I need to market my wedding business on TikTok?			</a>
		</h2>
		<p>
			<p>Every wedding vendor eventually asks the same exhausted question: “Do I need to be on TikTok?” Not because they want to be, but because guilt is a hell of a motivator. Here&#8217;s a reality check about temperament, energy, and whether performing for the algorithm actually makes sense for how you work&#8230; or whether it just sounds like torment. (And not the <a href="https://offbeatwed.com/tag/bdsm/">fun kind</a>!)</p>
		</p>
		<a href="https://offbeatwed.com/do-i-need-to-market-my-wedding-business-on-tiktok/">

	<div class="grid-item-details">
				<h2 class="grid-title">
			<a href="https://offbeatwed.com/gothic-elopement-scotland/">
				An LGBTQ+ gothic elopement in the Scottish woods (&#8230;WITH FIRE!)			</a>
		</h2>
		<p>
			<p>Kendal and Lake skipped the wedding industrial complex and went straight into the woods. From Alabama to a storm-soaked corner of Perthshire, Scotland they built an elopement around fire, water, moss, and intention. Gothic fashion, Celtic-inspired rituals, and a river vow sealed at dusk made this less a performance and more a reckoning with place, weather, and commitment.</p>
		</p>

			<a href="https://offbeatwed.com/how-to-get-found-by-chatgpt-a-free-tool-for-wedding-vendors/">
				How to get found by ChatGPT: a FREE tool for wedding vendors			</a>
		</h2>
		<p>
			<p>Couples are asking chatbots about wedding planning, and if machines can’t parse your business, you won&#8217;t appear in AI recommendations. <h2 class="wp-block-heading">We've been the web's home for nontraditional weddings since 2007</h2>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading">Offbeat Wed equips wedding professionals committed to nontraditional couples, publishing inclusive advice for the folks they serve.</h4>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">If you’re a wedding professional, welcome! We’ve built this part for you:</h5>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Grow your business with <a href="/join">education, tools, and industry insights</a>.</li>



<li>Learn how to use <a href="https://offbeatempire.gumroad.com/l/AI-for-wedding-pros" data-type="link" data-id="https://offbeatempire.gumroad.com/l/AI-for-wedding-pros" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">AI ethically and intelligently in your work</a></li>



<li>Build a more <a href="https://offbeatempire.gumroad.com/l/inclusive-marketing" target="_blank" rel="noopener">inclusive, values-aligned wedding business</a> that attracts the right couples</li>
</ul>



<h5 class="wp-block-heading">If you’re planning a wedding, you’re also in the right place. Start here:</h5>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Get organized with <a href="/wedding-spreadsheets">wedding planning spreadsheets and checklists</a></li>



<li>Browse <a href="https://offbeatwed.com/filed/ceremony-advice/wedding-ceremony-scripts/">wedding ceremony scripts</a> and <a href="https://offbeatwed.com/filed/ceremony-advice/wedding-vow-examples/">vow examples</a> (or <a href="/officiantpack" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">get help officiating a friend's wedding</a>!)</li>



<li>Find <a href="https://offbeatwed.com/wedding-vendors">inclusive wedding vendors</a> who align with your values </li>
</ul>

<h4 class="wp-block-heading">The backstory</h4>
</div><div>
<p>We originally launched as Offbeat Bride in January 2007, supporting the release of&nbsp;<a href="https://offbeatempire.com/about-ariel-meadow-stallings" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Ariel Meadow Stallings</a>' <a href="https://amzn.to/3H1BB72">book</a>. Then we wrote over&nbsp;<a href="https://mail.google.com/archive">7k posts</a>&nbsp;and helped&nbsp;<em>100 million</em>&nbsp;nontraditional folks plan weddings full of intention and personality. We changed our name to Offbeat Wed in 2022, because ew: gender norms. (...In this economy!?)</p>
</div><div>
<p>These days, we're mostly focused on <a href="/join">working with wedding vendors</a> to build their businesses.</p>
</div><div><p class="has-text-align-center"><button class="btn btn-primary"><a align="center" href="/about" target="new" rel="noopener"><b>OUR LORE</b></a></button></p></div>				</div>
